 function getSecondLevelDomainFromHostname(hostname) {
 var hostnameParts = hostname.split('.');
 if (hostnameParts.length < 2) {
 // hostname is toplevel domain
 return hostname;
 }
 return hostnameParts[hostnameParts.length-2] + "." + hostnameParts[hostnameParts.length-1];
 }
 function isReferrerFromSameSecondLevelDomain() {
 var referrer = document.referrer;
 if (!referrer) {
 return false;
 }
 var referrerSecondLevelDomain = getSecondLevelDomainFromHostname(new URL(referrer).hostname);
 var currentSecondLevelDomain = getSecondLevelDomainFromHostname(window.location.hostname);
 return referrerSecondLevelDomain === currentSecondLevelDomain;
 }
 function isMobileSwitchActive() {
 return ((!isMobilePage && isMobileUserAgent()) || (isMobilePage && !isMobileUserAgent())) && !isReferrerFromSameSecondLevelDomain();
 }
 function doMobileSwitchRedirect(isCausedDirectlyByPopupClick) {
 var redirectUrl = "https://mobil.rheinische-anzeigenblaetter.de/mein-blatt/bruehler-schlossbote";
 if (redirectUrl.indexOf("?") == -1) {
 // no queryparams found
 redirectUrl = redirectUrl + "?";
 } else {
 redirectUrl = redirectUrl + "&";
 }
 redirectUrl = redirectUrl + "originalReferrer=" + encodeURI(document.referrer);
 if (location.search !== "") {
 redirectUrl = redirectUrl + "&" + location.search.replace("?","");
 }
 if (isCausedDirectlyByPopupClick === true) {
 redirectUrl = redirectUrl + "&mobileSwitchPopupClick=1";
 }
 window.location.replace(redirectUrl);
 }
 function getCookieValueForMobileSwitch(name) {
 var nameWithEqualSign = name + "=";
 var cookieParts = document.cookie.split(';');
 for(var i=0; i < cookieParts.length; i++) {
 var cookiePart = cookieParts[i];
 while (cookiePart.charAt(0)==' ') cookiePart = cookiePart.substring(1);
 if (cookiePart.indexOf(nameWithEqualSign) == 0) return cookiePart.substring(nameWithEqualSign.length,cookiePart.length);
 }
 return "";
 }
 function setCookieForMobileSwitch(name, value, exdays) {
 var d = new Date();
 d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
 var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
 document.cookie = name + "=" + value + "; " + expires + "; domain=." + getSecondLevelDomainFromHostname(window.location.hostname) + "; path=/";
 }
 function setCookieMobileSwitchPreferred(value) {
 setCookieForMobileSwitch("mobileSwitchPreferred", value, 14);
 }
 var isMobilePage = false;
 if (isMobileSwitchActive()) {
 doMobileSwitchRedirect(false);
 }

       function createCookie(name, value, days) {
 if (days) {
 var date = new Date();
 date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
 var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 }
 else var expires = "";
 document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 }
 function readCookie(name) {
 var nameEQ = name + "=";
 var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
 for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
 var c = ca[i];
 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
 if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
 }
 return null;
 }
 function eraseCookie(name) {
 createCookie(name, "", -1);
 }
 if (readCookie('dmnDevice')) {
 document.write("<a href=\"https://mobil.rheinische-anzeigenblaetter.de/mein-blatt/bruehler-schlossbote/--24405664\" onclick=\"eraseCookie('dmnDevice')\" style=\"color:white\">zur mobilen Version</a>");
 }
